AS FEES FOR APPRAISAL CARRIED OUT BY THE BANK, YOU ARE CALLED UPON TO PAY ONE-TIME NON-REFUNDABLE PROCESSING FEE EQUIVALENT TO 221000 INR (EXCLUSIVE OF GST AND STATUTORY LEVIES, IF ANY) BY WAY OF A CHEQUE / DEMAND DRAFT PAYABLE FAVOURING ICICI BANK LIMITED" AND / OR SUCH OTHER MODE AS MAY BE ACCEPTABLE TO ICICI BANK PLEASE NOTE THAT THIS COMMUNICATION SHOULD NOT BE CONSTRUED AS GIVING RISE TO ANY BINDING OBLIGATION ON THE PART OF ICICI BANK UNLESS THE BANK RECEIVES DUPLICATE COPY OF THIS LETTER,DULY SIGNED IN TOKEN OF ACCEPTANCE,WITHIN 150 DAYS FROM THE DATE OF SANCTION I.E. 29-MAY-2021 AND UNLESS AGREEMENTS / DOCUMENTS ARE SIGNED / EXECUTED IN RESPECT OF THE FACILITIES WITHIN 150 DAYS FROM THE DATE OF SANCTION I.E. 29-MAY-2021, THE OFFER SHALL AUTOMATICALLY LAPSE WITHOUT ANY FURTHER COMMUNICATION FROM THE BANK, UNLESS THE VALIDITY OF THE OFFER IS EXPRESSLY EXTENDED / REVIVED BY THE BANK IN WRITING. THE BANK WITHOUT ASSIGNING ANY REASON RESERVES THE RIGHT TO NOT DISBURSE ANY FACILITIES PARTIALLY OR FULLY AND THE BORROWER / GUARANTORS SHALL NOT HAVE ANY CLAIM AGAINST THE BANK FOR SUCH NON DISBURSEMENT. THE APPLICABLE REPO RATE SHALL BE THE RATE PREVAILING ONE BUSINESS DAY PRECEDING THE DATE OF ACCOUNT OPENING /LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL. AS ON DATE THE REPO RATE IS 4% AND SPREAD IS 3.6% . *"REPO RATE" OR "POLICY REPO RATE" MEANS THE RATE OF INTEREST PUBLISHED BY THE RESERVE BANK OF INDIA ("RBI") ON, THE RBI WEBSITE FROM TIME TO TIME AS REPO RATE OR POLICY REPO RATE. THE REPO RATE COMPONENT OF THE INTEREST RATE SHALL BE RESET AFTER EVERY 3 MONTHS FOLLOWING THE DATE OF LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL (AS APPLICABLE), AS A SUM OF REPO RATE + "SPREAD", PLUS APPLICABLE STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY. THE APPLICABLE REPO RATE SHALL BE THE RATE PREVAILING ONE BUSINESS DAY PRECEDING THE RESET DATE. * * ** ILLUSTRATION: FOR ACCOUNT OPENING /LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL DONE ON OCTOBER 5 2019 THE FIRST RESET DATE WILL BE JANUARY 5, 2020 AND THEREAFTER ON APRIL 5, 2020 AND SO ON. THE BORROWER FURTHER ACKNOWLEDGES THAT INTEREST RATE MAY CHANGE, UPWARD OR DOWNWARDS, AS THE CASE MAY BE, IN LINE WITH CHANGE IN THE REPO RATE. THE BANK RESERVES THE RIGHT TO RESET THE SPREAD AT ANY TIME UPON SUBSTANTIAL CHANGE IN THE BORROWER'S CREDIT ASSESSMENT AND/ OR ON ACCOUNT OF DETERIORATION IN THE CREDIT RISK PROFILE. ANY CHANGE IN 'SPREAD' WOULD BE COMMUNICATED BY THE BANK THROUGH EITHER: (I) LETTER (II) E-MAIL (III) SMS (IV) STATEMENTS OF ACCOUNTS (V) WHATSAPP OR ANY OTHER SUITABLE MODE. THE APPLICABLE REPO RATE SHALL BE THE RATE PREVAILING ONE BUSINESS DAY PRECEDING THE DATE OF ACCOUNT OPENING /LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL. AS ON DATE THE REPO RATE IS 4% AND SPREAD IS 3.6% . *"REPO RATE" OR "POLICY REPO RATE" MEANS THE RATE OF INTEREST PUBLISHED BY THE RESERVE BANK OF INDIA ("RBI") ON, THE RBI WEBSITE FROM TIME TO TIME AS REPO RATE OR POLICY REPO RATE. THE REPO RATE COMPONENT OF THE INTEREST RATE SHALL BE RESET AFTER EVERY 3 MONTHS FOLLOWING THE DATE OF LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL (AS APPLICABLE), AS A SUM OF REPO RATE + "SPREAD", PLUS APPLICABLE STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY. THE APPLICABLE REPO RATE SHALL BE THE RATE PREVAILING ONE BUSINESS DAY PRECEDING THE RESET DATE. * * ** ILLUSTRATION: FOR ACCOUNT OPENING /LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL DONE ON OCTOBER 5 2019 THE FIRST RESET DATE WILL BE JANUARY 5, 2020 AND THEREAFTER ON APRIL 5, 2020 AND SO ON. THE BANK SHALL HAVE THE RIGHT TO MODIFY THE RESET FREQUENCY AND RESET DATE FROM TIME TO TIME IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE EXTANT RBI GUIDELINES. THE BORROWER FURTHER ACKNOWLEDGES THAT INTEREST RATE MAY CHANGE, UPWARD OR DOWNWARDS, AS THE CASE MAY BE, IN LINE WITH CHANGE IN THE REPO RATE. THE BANK RESERVES THE RIGHT TO RESET THE SPREAD AT ANY TIME UPON SUBSTANTIAL CHANGE IN THE BORROWER'S CREDIT ASSESSMENT AND/ OR ON ACCOUNT OF DETERIORATION IN THE CREDIT RISK PROFILE. ANY CHANGE IN 'SPREAD' WOULD BE COMMUNICATED BY THE BANK THROUGH EITHER: (I) LETTER (II) E-MAIL (III) SMS (IV) STATEMENTS OF ACCOUNTS (V) WHATSAPP OR ANY OTHER SUITABLE MODE. THE BORROWER SHALL BE DEEMED TO HAVE NOTICE OF CHANGES IN THE REPO RATE WHEN DISPLAYED ON THE NOTICE BOARD OF THE BRANCH OR DISPLAYED ON BANKS WEBSITE (WWW.ICICIBANK.COM) AND THE BORROWER IS LIABLE TO PAY SUCH REVISED RATE OF INTEREST. THE APPLICABLE REPO RATE SHALL BE THE RATE PREVAILING ONE BUSINESS DAY PRECEDING THE DATE OF ACCOUNT OPENING /LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL. AS ON DATE THE REPO RATE IS 4% AND SPREAD IS 3.6% . *"REPO RATE" OR "POLICY REPO RATE" MEANS THE RATE OF INTEREST PUBLISHED BY THE RESERVE BANK OF INDIA ("RBI") ON, THE RBI WEBSITE FROM TIME TO TIME AS REPO RATE OR POLICY REPO RATE. THE REPO RATE COMPONENT OF THE INTEREST RATE SHALL BE RESET AFTER EVERY 3 MONTHS FOLLOWING THE DATE OF LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL (AS APPLICABLE), AS A SUM OF REPO RATE + "SPREAD", PLUS APPLICABLE STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY. THE APPLICABLE REPO RATE SHALL BE THE RATE PREVAILING ONE BUSINESS DAY PRECEDING THE RESET DATE. * * ** ILLUSTRATION: FOR ACCOUNT OPENING /LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL DONE ON OCTOBER 5 2019 THE FIRST RESET DATE WILL BE JANUARY 5, 2020 AND THEREAFTER ON APRIL 5, 2020 AND SO ON. THE BORROWER FURTHER ACKNOWLEDGES THAT INTEREST RATE MAY CHANGE, UPWARD OR DOWNWARDS, AS THE CASE MAY BE, IN LINE WITH CHANGE IN THE REPO RATE. THE BANK RESERVES THE RIGHT TO RESET THE SPREAD AT ANY TIME UPON SUBSTANTIAL CHANGE IN THE BORROWER'S CREDIT ASSESSMENT AND/ OR ON ACCOUNT OF DETERIORATION IN THE CREDIT RISK PROFILE. THE REPO RATE COMPONENT OF THE INTEREST RATE SHALL BE RESET AFTER EVERY 3 MONTHS FOLLOWING THE DATE OF LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL (AS APPLICABLE), AS A SUM OF REPO RATE + "SPREAD", PLUS APPLICABLE STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY. AS ON DATE THE REPO RATE IS 4% AND SPREAD IS 3.6% . *"REPO RATE" OR "POLICY REPO RATE" MEANS THE RATE OF INTEREST PUBLISHED BY THE RESERVE BANK OF INDIA ("RBI") ON, THE RBI WEBSITE FROM TIME TO TIME AS REPO RATE OR POLICY REPO RATE. THE REPO RATE COMPONENT OF THE INTEREST RATE SHALL BE RESET AFTER EVERY 3 MONTHS FOLLOWING THE DATE OF LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL (AS APPLICABLE), AS A SUM OF REPO RATE + "SPREAD", PLUS APPLICABLE STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY. THE REPO RATE COMPONENT OF THE INTEREST RATE SHALL BE RESET AFTER EVERY 3 MONTHS FOLLOWING THE DATE OF LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL (AS APPLICABLE), AS A SUM OF REPO RATE + "SPREAD", PLUS APPLICABLE STATUTORY LEVY, IF ANY. THE APPLICABLE REPO RATE SHALL BE THE RATE PREVAILING ONE BUSINESS DAY PRECEDING THE RESET DATE. * * ** ILLUSTRATION: FOR ACCOUNT OPENING /LIMIT SET-UP /RENEWAL DONE ON OCTOBER 5 2019 THE FIRST RESET DATE WILL BE JANUARY 5, 2020 AND THEREAFTER ON APRIL 5, 2020 AND SO ON. THE BANK SHALL HAVE THE RIGHT TO MODIFY THE RESET FREQUENCY AND RESET DATE FROM TIME TO TIME IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE EXTANT RBI GUIDELINES. THE BORROWER FURTHER ACKNOWLEDGES THAT INTEREST RATE MAY CHANGE, UPWARD OR DOWNWARDS, AS THE CASE MAY BE, IN LINE WITH CHANGE IN THE REPO RATE. THE BANK RESERVES THE RIGHT TO RESET THE SPREAD AT ANY TIME UPON SUBSTANTIAL CHANGE IN THE BORROWER'S CREDIT ASSESSMENT AND/ OR ON ACCOUNT OF DETERIORATION IN THE CREDIT RISK PROFILE. ANY CHANGE IN 'SPREAD' WOULD BE COMMUNICATED BY THE BANK THROUGH EITHER: (I) LETTER (II) E-MAIL (III) SMS (IV) STATEMENTS OF ACCOUNTS (V) WHATSAPP OR ANY OTHER SUITABLE MODE. THE BORROWER SHALL BE DEEMED TO HAVE NOTICE OF CHANGES IN THE REPO RATE WHEN DISPLAYED ON THE NOTICE BOARD OF THE BRANCH OR DISPLAYED ON BANKS WEBSITE (WWW.ICICIBANK.COM) AND THE BORROWER IS LIABLE TO PAY SUCH REVISED RATE OF INTEREST.
